like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . tell your doctor or pharmacist as soon as possible if you notice any of the following serious side effects : very common side effects ( may affect more than 1 in 10 people ): - infections ( which may affect up to 1 in 10 people ) - infection with signs such as fever , fever , infection , infections , - fever , - fever , signs of infection or fever , - fever , signs of infection or fever , - fever , signs of infection or fever , - fever , signs of infection or fever , - fever , signs of infection or extreme tiredness . these may be due to rare decrease of some blood cells . - signs of infection or fever , especially if you had fever , signs of infection or other signs of infection ( since you might have less white blood cells than normal which is very common ). if you experience bleeding from the gums , tell your doctor straight away . reporting of side effects if you get any side effects , talk to your doctor or pharmacist . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine .
